# AuditIQ Master Bible Requirements Traceability Audit

This document provides a mathematically derived, strictly evidence-based Requirement Traceability Matrix against the original AuditIQ Master Project Bible v1.0. Every requirement has been verified across the source code, documentation, UI, pipeline, and execution levels.

## Master Bible

### Blueprint V1

#### Section 11.1

**Requirement 11.1.1**

**Status:**

FAIL

**Traceability Chain:**
Bible Requirement (✅) ↓ Blueprint Requirement (✅) ↓ Source Code (❌) ↓ UI (❌) ↓ Localhost (❌) ↓ Test Dataset (❌) ↓ Documentation (❌) ↓ Compliance (FAIL)
